Logiwa OpenAPI v3.1
Logiwa Open API
 v3.1 
OAS 3.0
/swagger/v3.1/swagger.json
Overview
Logiwa offers a suite of APIs that allow developers to extend the platform’s built-in features. These APIs enable partners to read and write data, as well as interoperate with other systems and platforms.

Base URLs
Sandbox: https://myapisandbox.logiwa.com
Production: https://myapi.logiwa.com
API Versioning
The endpoints in this document belong to version 3.1 unless otherwise specified. Endpoints belonging to different versions are specified in the section header of each endpoint (e.g., Version: v3.2 or Version: v3.3). Please ensure that you send the correct version number in the API requests you create.

Rate Limits
To ensure the stability and reliability of our API for all users, we implement rate limiting on the number of requests that can be made within a specific period.

Standard Endpoint Rate Limits:
Basic Tier Users: Limited to 2 requests per second.
Premium Tier Users: Allowed up to 6 requests per second.
Bulk Endpoint Rate Limits:
Bulk endpoints allow operations on multiple resources in a single request. A single bulk request can include a maximum of 50 objects.

Basic Tier Users: Limited to 1 bulk request every 6 seconds.
Premium Tier Users: Allowed 1 bulk request every 2 seconds.
While the above outlines our general rate-limiting policies, individual API endpoints may have additional, more specific limitations. Such information will be provided in the relevant section of the endpoint documentation.

Logiwa Query Language (LQL)
Many of our API endpoints support advanced filtering capabilities through the Logiwa Query Language (LQL). LQL allows you to construct powerful queries to retrieve specific datasets, enhancing the flexibility of your API interactions.

LQL queries are appended to the endpoint URL as a query string, starting after the question mark (?). The basic structure of an LQL filter is:

{fieldName}.{LQL_aggregator}={value}

Multiple LQL filters can be combined using the ampersand (&) character.

Example Endpoint Structure:

https://{subdomain}.logiwa.com/v{version}/{operationGroup}/i/{startIndex}/s/{pageSize}?{LQL_query}

LQL Aggregators
Aggregator	Description	Example Usage
gt	Greater Than	CreatedDate.gt=2024-01-01
gte	Greater Than or Equal To	Quantity.gte=10
lt	Less Than	Price.lt=50.00
lte	Less Than or Equal To	Weight.lte=2.5
eq	Equal To	Status.eq=Active
bt	Between (inclusive)	OrderDate.bt=2024-01-01,2024-01-31
Available Query Parameters
All fields that can be used for LQL filtering are listed as query parameters on their respective endpoints within this Swagger documentation. If an endpoint does not display any query parameters, it indicates that filtering via LQL is not supported for that specific method.

Filter Value Types
LQL supports various data types for filter values, including but not limited to:

Date: YYYY-MM-DD (e.g., 2024-03-04)
String: Case-sensitive (e.g., NI-HS0923-27022024A)
Identifier (GUID/UUID): e.g., 7546ad2f-81d1-4308-b744-2e29af43fc16
Numeric: Integers or decimals (e.g., 10, 49.99)
LQL Query Example:
Retrieve serial tracking data created between March 4th and March 5th, 2024, for a specific purchase order, SKU, client, warehouse, serial number, and status.

https://myapi.logiwa.com/v3.1/Report/SerialTracking/i/0/s/200?CreatedDate.bt=2024-03-04,2024-03-05&PurchaseOrderNumber.eq=NI-HS0923-27022024A&SKU.eq=HD_APPLE_WATCH_SE2_44MM_Silver_Blue&ClientIdentifier.eq=7546ad2f-81d1-4308-b744-2e29af43fc16&WarehouseIdentifier.eq=4b8aa8cc-2685-4cbd-87c6-4fa90c14b70c&PrimarySerialNumber.eq=sf702dqv4m0&SerialStatusName.eq=Received

Below is a list of available webhooks to which you can subscribe:

wms/mobilecart/update
NOTE: When using a webhook, we recommend calling the necessary endpoint from the API at regular intervals to check for missing information flow.

HTTP Status Codes
Status Code	Description	What It Means
200 OK	The request was successful.	
201 Created	The POST request was successful, and the entity has been returned in the response.	
204 No Content	The GET request was successful, and there is no content in the response.	
400 Bad Request	The request was malformed and could not be processed.	If making an authorization request, this may mean the Token is not accurate.
401 Unauthorized	The token provided is either invalid or expired.	The token was not provided in the correct manner, or does not provide sufficient privileges for the action requested.
404 Not Found	Either the URL format is invalid, or an entity with the specified ID does not exist.	
413 Request Entity Too Large	The length of the request content has exceeded the maximum allowed limit.	
414 Request URI Too Long	The length of the request URI has exceeded the maximum allowed limit.	
415 Unsupported Media Type	The request media type/format is not supported.	(e.g., Content-Type value doesn't align with what is expected.)
429 Too Many Requests	A rate limit has been exceeded, resulting in the request being throttled.	
500 Internal Server Error	A system error occurred while processing the request.	If this situation persists, please open a support case.
503 Service Unavailable	The API is currently unavailable due to maintenance.

ShipmentOrder
Shipment Order endpoints is used for managing Shipment Orders. Both command and query endpoints are listed.
